				="综合判断对象"	="不包含在综合判断内"

			="个别设定"
				="计算公式"	="#SuccessCalc1 = 0"
				=""	=""
				=""	="#Corner_A.X = 0"
				=""	="#Corner_A.Y = 0"
				=""	=""
				=""	="#Corner_A = ISect(!U[0044].RSLT.DLRTH:MS, !U[0004].RSLT.DLRTH:MS)"
				=""	=""
				=""	="#Corner_A_Grid = ConvPixToWld(#Corner_A, !U[0017].RSLT.CALIB[])"
				=""	=""
				=""	="#ThetaCam1 = ConvPixToWld(#Corner_A, !U[0017].RSLT.CALIB[])"
				=""	=""
				=""	="#edge_intensity_A1 = 0   'For calculation average intensity of detected segments"
				=""	="@counter = 0"
				=""	="@temp_value = 0"
				=""	="#number_segments = 0"
				=""	="DO WHILE @counter < 100"
				=""	="    @temp_value = !U[0002].RSLT.I[@counter]:MS     "
				=""	="    IF @temp_value <> 0 THEN"
				=""	="        #edge_intensity_A1 = (#edge_intensity_A1*#number_segments)+@temp_value"
				=""	="        #number_segments = #number_segments + 1"
				=""	="        #edge_intensity_A1 = #edge_intensity_A1 / #number_segments"
				=""	="    ENDIF"
				=""	="    @counter = @counter + 1"
				=""	="LOOP"
				=""	=""
				=""	="'Calculate average distance between detected pixel and best fit line. "
				=""	="'#number_segments = 0"
				=""	="'#Distance = 0"
				=""	="'#Average_Distance = 0"
				=""	="'FOR @A = 0 TO !U[0002].RSLT.SGN:MS"
				=""	="'    IF !U[0002].RSLT.X[@A]:MS <> 0 THEN"
				=""	="'        #Distance = LnDist(!U[0002].RSLT.DLRTH:MS, !U[0002].RSLT.XY[@A]:MS) 'Distance between best fit line and detected pixel"
				=""	="'        #Average_Distance = ((#Average_Distance * #number_segments)+#Distance)/(#number_segments+1)"
				=""	="'        #number_segments = #number_segments + 1"
				=""	="'    ENDIF"
				=""	="'NEXT"
				=""	=""
				=""	="IF !U[0044].RSLT.N[JGL]:MS > 0 AND !U[0004].RSLT.N[JGL]:MS > 0 THEN"
				=""	="    #SuccessCalc1 = 1"
				=""	="ENDIF"
				=""	=""

				="计算结果：下限"	="(未设定)"
				="超时间隔"	="1s"
